        <h2 style="text-align: center;">
         February Round Robin Giveaway
        </h2>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         This giveaway is now expired. Be sure to check out the
         <a href="http://smslwithheidi.com/giveaways">
          giveaways
         </a>
         and the
         <a href="http://smslwithheidi.com/giveaways/giveaways-linky">
          giveaway linky
         </a>
         for more great giveaways for you to enter to win!
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://smslwithheidi.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/10952571_10153012430810977_3326843829087335310_n.jpg">
          <img alt="February Round Robin Giveaway" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-131260" height="500" src="http://smslwithheidi.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/10952571_10153012430810977_3326843829087335310_n.jpg" width="500"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         We have officially survived January and February is well underway! February is a very busy month for the SMSL household, but I wanted to be sure to bring you a chance to win this month! I am offering a $15 Paypal Cash prize and then you can travel around to the other sites and enter to win their $15 prizes too!! There is a total of $300 up for grabs so be sure you get entered to win!
        </p>
        <p>
         Each blogger is offering a $15 prize that includes gift cards, Paypal Cash, Amazon cash and lots of great stores. Some of the stores include iTunes, CVS, Starbucks, Paypal, Amazon Cash and many more!
        </p>
        <p>
         How to enter for a $15 Paypal Cash prize!!!
        </p>
        <p>
         Entry details
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Leave me a comment-What is your favorite thing about February or Valentines Day?
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://eepurl.com/T9dgj">
          Sign up for my email newsletter
         </a>
         Leave me a comment below telling me you signed up. (Make sure you confirm your subscription.)
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/SaveMreSpendLes/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          Follow me on Pinterest
         </a>
         : Be sure you come back and leave me your Pinterest username too!
        </p>
        <p>
         Because this is a Round Robin Giveaway you have several chances to win some great prizes!!
        </p>
        <p>
         After you leave me a comment, head over to visit: This and That With Oliviafor a $15 AmazonCash prize! The more blogs you visit the better chance you have to win! Good luck!
        </p>

        </p>
        <p>
         Giveaway Details:
        </p>
        <p>
         Starts: February 9, 2015
        </p>
        <p>
         Ends: February 20, 2015
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Winner will be randomly selected by Random.org. All entries will be verified and giveaway is open to US residents. Winner will have 24 hours to claim their prize or I will pick a new winner. 3 entries max per person. Save More Spend Less with Heidi is only responsible for 1 $15 Paypal Prize. All other prizes will be filled by participating bloggers.
         </strong>
        </p>

          <div class="comment-content" itemprop="commentText">
           <p>
            Groundhog Day (February 2) is my favorite thing about February. Its not just one in a number of great Bill Murray flicks of the 20th century, but its also a flawless meteorological technique done by a plump porcupine-looking varmint that is likely rabid and obese, a clear mascot for America.
           </p>
          </div>
